(*******************************************************************

 The trivial comprehension bicategory

 If we have a bicategory with products, then we obtain a
 comprehension bicategory. The fibration comes from the trivial
 displayed bicategory and for the comprehension pseudofunctor, we
 use that the bicategory has products.

 Contents
 1. The comprehension pseudofunctor
 2. Preservation of cartesian 1-cells
 3. Preservation of (op)cartesian 2-cells
 4. The comprehension bicategory

 *******************************************************************)

            (unfold coherent_homot ;
             cbn ;

             etrans ;

               rewrite !vassocr ;
               rewrite lassociator_rassociator ;
               rewrite id2_left ;
               apply idpath
             | ] ;
             etrans ;
             [ do 3 apply maponpaths ;
               rewrite !vassocr ;
               rewrite lwhisker_vcomp ;
               rewrite vcomp_linv ;
               rewrite lwhisker_id2 ;

               apply idpath
             | ] ;
             etrans ;
             [ do 2 apply maponpaths ;
               rewrite !vassocr ;
               rewrite rassociator_lassociator ;
               rewrite id2_left ;
               apply idpath

               rewrite !vassocr ;
               rewrite rwhisker_vcomp ;
               rewrite vcomp_linv ;
               rewrite id2_rwhisker ;
               rewrite id2_left ;
               apply idpath

             rewrite lassociator_rassociator ;
             rewrite lwhisker_id2 ;
             apply idpath).

              (♯ trivial_comprehension_data ff)
              (♯ trivial_comprehension_data gg)
              (♯ trivial_comprehension_data hh))
           (disp_rwhisker
              (♯ trivial_comprehension_data hh)
              (disp_psfunctor_comp
                 (trivial_displayed_bicat B B)
                 (cod_disp_bicat B) (id_psfunctor B)
                 trivial_comprehension_data ff gg)))
        (disp_psfunctor_comp
           (trivial_displayed_bicat B B)
           (cod_disp_bicat B) (id_psfunctor B)
           trivial_comprehension_data
           (Core.comp_disp ff gg) hh)))
 
B: bicat_with_binprod
a, b, c, d: B
f: B ⟦ a, b ⟧
g: B ⟦ b, c ⟧
h: B ⟦ c, d ⟧
aa: Core.ob_disp
  (Core.disp_cat_ob_mor_from_disp_cat_data

  (disp_vcomp2

     (♯♯ trivial_comprehension_data
        (disp_lassociator ff gg hh))) =

  (disp_vcomp2
     (disp_vcomp2

        (trivial_displayed_bicat B B)

    apply binprod_lassociator.
  
B: bicat_with_binprod

f: B ⟦ a, b ⟧

  (Core.disp_cat_ob_mor_from_disp_cat_data

  (disp_vcomp2
     (disp_psfunctor_comp
        (trivial_displayed_bicat B B)
        (cod_disp_bicat B) (id_psfunctor B)

     (λ p : Functors.functor_on_morphisms
              (id_psfunctor B) f
            · Functors.functor_on_morphisms
                (id_psfunctor B) g₁ ==>
            Functors.functor_on_morphisms
              (id_psfunctor B) (f · g₂),

        (Core.comp_disp

           (♯ trivial_comprehension_data gg₁))
        (♯ trivial_comprehension_data
           (Core.comp_disp ff gg₂)))
     (psfunctor_lwhisker (id_psfunctor B) f η)
     (disp_vcomp2
        (disp_lwhisker
           (♯ trivial_comprehension_data ff)
           (♯♯ trivial_comprehension_data ηη))
        (disp_psfunctor_comp
           (trivial_displayed_bicat B B)
           (cod_disp_bicat B) (id_psfunctor B)
           trivial_comprehension_data ff gg₂)))

  Defined.

  (**
   2. Preservation of cartesian 1-cells
   *)
  Section GlobalCartesian.
    Context {b₁ b₂ : B}
            (f : b₁ --> b₂)
            {c₁ c₂ : B}
            (l : c₁ --> c₂)
            (Hl : left_adjoint_equivalence l).

    Let cone : pb_cone f π₁
      := make_pb_cone
           (b₁ ⊗ c₁)
           π₁
           (f ⊗₁ l)
           (inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)).

    Let r : c₂ --> c₁
      := left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl.
    Let η : invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁) (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
      := left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl.
    Let ε : invertible_2cell (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) (id₁ c₂)
      := left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl.

    Section AdjEquivToUMP1.
      Context (q : pb_cone f (π₁ : b₂ ⊗ c₂ --> b₂)).

      Local Definition adj_equiv_to_pb_ump_1_pb_1cell_map
        : q --> b₁ ⊗ c₁
        := ⟨ pb_cone_pr1 q , pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂ · r ⟩.

      Local Notation "'φ'" := adj_equiv_to_pb_ump_1_pb_1cell_map.

      Local Definition adj_equiv_to_pb_ump_1_pb_1cell_π₁
        : invertible_2cell (φ · π₁) (pb_cone_pr1 q)
        := prod_1cell_pr1 _ _ _.

      Local Notation "'φπ₁'" := adj_equiv_to_pb_ump_1_pb_1cell_π₁.

      Local Definition adj_equiv_to_pb_ump_1_pb_1cell_cell_π₁
        : φ · (f ⊗₁ l) · π₁ ==> pb_cone_pr2 q · π₁
        := rassociator _ _ _
           • (_ ◃ pair_1cell_pr1 _ _ _)
           • lassociator _ _ _
           • (prod_1cell_pr1 _ _ _ ▹ _)
           • pb_cone_cell _.

      Local Notation "'φπ₂_cell_π₁'" := adj_equiv_to_pb_ump_1_pb_1cell_cell_π₁.

      Local Definition adj_equiv_to_pb_ump_1_pb_1cell_cell_π₂
        : φ · (f ⊗₁ l) · π₂ ==> pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂
        := rassociator _ _ _
           • (_ ◃ pair_1cell_pr2 _ _ _)
           • lassociator _ _ _
           • (prod_1cell_pr2 _ _ _ ▹ _)
           • rassociator _ _ _
           • (_ ◃ ε)
           • runitor _.

      Local Notation "'φπ₂_cell_π₂'" := adj_equiv_to_pb_ump_1_pb_1cell_cell_π₂.

r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)
q: pb_cone f (π₁ : B ⟦ b₂ ⊗ c₂, b₂ ⟧)
φ · (f ⊗₁ l) ==> pb_cone_pr2 q

      Local Notation "'φπ₂'" := adj_equiv_to_pb_ump_1_pb_1cell_invcell.

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
l: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ (f ⊗₁ l)
(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)
q: pb_cone f (π₁ : B ⟦ b₂ ⊗ c₂, b₂ ⟧)
φ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone =
(((lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f • (φπ₁ ▹ f))
  • pb_cone_cell q) • (φπ₂ ^-1 ▹ π₁))
• rassociator φ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
l: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ (f ⊗₁ l)
(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)
q: pb_cone f (π₁ : B ⟦ b₂ ⊗ c₂, b₂ ⟧)
φ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone =
(((lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f • (φπ₁ ▹ f))
  • pb_cone_cell q) • (φπ₂ ^-1 ▹ π₁))
• rassociator φ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁

        
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B

Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ (f ⊗₁ l)
(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)

  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)
q: pb_cone f (π₁ : B ⟦ b₂ ⊗ c₂, b₂ ⟧)
φ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l) ^-1 =
(((lassociator φ π₁ f • (φπ₁ ▹ f)) • pb_cone_cell q)
 • (binprod_ump_2cell (pr2 (binprod_of B b₂ c₂))
      ((pr2 (pb_cone_cell q)) ^-1
       • (((pr2
              (prod_1cell_pr1 B (pb_cone_pr1 q)
                 (pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂ · r))) ^-1 ▹ f)
          • (rassociator
               ⟨ pb_cone_pr1 q, pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂ · r
               ⟩ π₁ f
             • ((⟨ pb_cone_pr1 q,
                 pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂ · r ⟩
                 ◃ (pr2 (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)) ^-1)
                • lassociator
                    ⟨ pb_cone_pr1 q,
                    pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂ · r ⟩ (f ⊗₁ l)
                    π₁))))
      (rinvunitor (pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂)
       • ((pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂ ◃ (pr222 Hl) ^-1)
          • (lassociator (pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂)
               (left_adjoint_right_adjoint (pr1 Hl)) l
             • (((pr2
                    (prod_1cell_pr2 B (pb_cone_pr1 q)
                       (pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂
                        · left_adjoint_right_adjoint
                            (pr1 Hl)))) ^-1 ▹ l)
                • (rassociator
                     ⟨ pb_cone_pr1 q,
                     pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂
                     · left_adjoint_right_adjoint
                         (pr1 Hl) ⟩ π₂ l
                   • ((⟨ pb_cone_pr1 q,
                       pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂
                       · left_adjoint_right_adjoint
                           (pr1 Hl) ⟩
                       ◃ (pr2 (pair_1cell_pr2 B f l))
                         ^-1)
                      • lassociator
                          ⟨ pb_cone_pr1 q,
                          pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂
                          · left_adjoint_right_adjoint
                              (pr1 Hl) ⟩ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂))))))
    ▹ π₁)) • rassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₁

(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)
q: pb_cone f (π₁ : B ⟦ b₂ ⊗ c₂, b₂ ⟧)
lassociator φ π₁ f
• ((φπ₁ ▹ f)
   • (pb_cone_cell q
      • ((pr2 (pb_cone_cell q)) ^-1
         • (((pr2
                (prod_1cell_pr1 B (pb_cone_pr1 q)
                   (pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂ · r))) ^-1 ▹ f)
            • (rassociator
                 ⟨ pb_cone_pr1 q,
                 pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂ · r ⟩ π₁ f
               • ((⟨ pb_cone_pr1 q,
                   pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂ · r ⟩
                   ◃ (pr2 (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)) ^-1)
                  • (lassociator
                       ⟨ pb_cone_pr1 q,
                       pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂ · r ⟩
                       (f ⊗₁ l) π₁
                     • rassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₁))))))) =
φ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l) ^-1

f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
l: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ (f ⊗₁ l)
(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)
q: pb_cone f (π₁ : B ⟦ b₂ ⊗ c₂, b₂ ⟧)
(((φπ₁
   • (pr2
        (prod_1cell_pr1 B (pb_cone_pr1 q)
           (pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂ · r))) ^-1) ▹ f)
 • rassociator
     ⟨ pb_cone_pr1 q, pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂ · r ⟩ π₁ f)
• (⟨ pb_cone_pr1 q, pb_cone_pr2 q · π₂ · r ⟩
   ◃ (pr2 (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)) ^-1) = ?t2

pb_1cell q cone

      exact (adj_equiv_to_pb_ump_1_pb_1cell q).
    Defined.

    Section AdjEquivToUMP2.
      Context {q : B}
              {φ ψ : q --> cone}
              (α : φ · pb_cone_pr1 cone ==> ψ · pb_cone_pr1 cone)
              (β : φ · pb_cone_pr2 cone ==> ψ · pb_cone_pr2 cone)
              (p : (φ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
                   • lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁
                   • (β ▹ π₁)
                   • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁
                   =
                   lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f
                   • (α ▹ f)
                   • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f
                   • (ψ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)).

      Let φπ₂ : φ · π₂ ==> ψ · π₂
        := fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map
             (adj_equiv_fully_faithful Hl)
             (rassociator φ π₂ l
              • (φ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr2 B f l) ^-1)
              • lassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂
              • (β ▹ π₂)
              • rassociator ψ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂
              • (ψ ◃ pair_1cell_pr2 B f l)
              • lassociator ψ π₂ l).

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
l: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ (f ⊗₁ l)
(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)
q: B
φ, ψ: B ⟦ q, cone ⟧
α: φ · pb_cone_pr1 cone ==> ψ · pb_cone_pr1 cone
β: φ · pb_cone_pr2 cone ==> ψ · pb_cone_pr2 cone
p: (((φ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
  • lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁)
 • (β ▹ π₁)) • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁ =
((lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f • (α ▹ f))
 • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f)
• (ψ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
φπ₂:= fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map
  (adj_equiv_fully_faithful Hl)
  ((((((rassociator φ π₂ l
        • (φ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr2 B f l) ^-1))
       • lassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂) • 
      (β ▹ π₂)) • rassociator ψ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂)
    • (ψ ◃ pair_1cell_pr2 B f l))
   • lassociator ψ π₂ l): φ · π₂ ==> ψ · π₂
isaprop
  (∑ γ : φ ==> ψ,
   γ ▹ pb_cone_pr1 cone = α × γ ▹ pb_cone_pr2 cone = β)

φ, ψ: B ⟦ q, cone ⟧
α: φ · pb_cone_pr1 cone ==> ψ · pb_cone_pr1 cone
β: φ · pb_cone_pr2 cone ==> ψ · pb_cone_pr2 cone
p: (((φ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
  • lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁)
 • (β ▹ π₁)) • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁ =
((lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f • (α ▹ f))
 • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f)
• (ψ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
φπ₂:= fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map
  (adj_equiv_fully_faithful Hl)
  ((((((rassociator φ π₂ l
        • (φ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr2 B f l) ^-1))
       • lassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂) • 
      (β ▹ π₂)) • rassociator ψ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂)
    • (ψ ◃ pair_1cell_pr2 B f l))
   • lassociator ψ π₂ l): φ · π₂ ==> ψ · π₂
ζ₁, ζ₂: ∑ γ : φ ==> ψ,
γ ▹ pb_cone_pr1 cone = α
× γ ▹ pb_cone_pr2 cone = β
φ · binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ c₁)) ==>
ψ · binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ c₁))
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
l: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ 
  (f ⊗₁ l)
  (inv_of_invertible_2cell
     (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)

φ, ψ: B ⟦ q, cone ⟧
α: φ · pb_cone_pr1 cone ==> ψ · pb_cone_pr1 cone
β: φ · pb_cone_pr2 cone ==> ψ · pb_cone_pr2 cone
p: (((φ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
  • lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁)
 • (β ▹ π₁)) • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁ =
((lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f • (α ▹ f))
 • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f)
• (ψ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
φπ₂:= fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map
  (adj_equiv_fully_faithful Hl)
  ((((((rassociator φ π₂ l
        • (φ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr2 B f l) ^-1))
       • lassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂) • 
      (β ▹ π₂)) • rassociator ψ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂)
    • (ψ ◃ pair_1cell_pr2 B f l))
   • lassociator ψ π₂ l): φ · π₂ ==> ψ · π₂
ζ₁, ζ₂: ∑ γ : φ ==> ψ,
γ ▹ pb_cone_pr1 cone = α
× γ ▹ pb_cone_pr2 cone = β
φπ₂ ▹ l =
(pr1 ζ₁ ▹ binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ c₁)))
▹ l

          
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
l: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ (f ⊗₁ l)
(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)

  • lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁)
 • (β ▹ π₁)) • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁ =
((lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f • (α ▹ f))
 • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f)
• (ψ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
φπ₂:= fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map
  (adj_equiv_fully_faithful Hl)
  ((((((rassociator φ π₂ l
        • (φ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr2 B f l) ^-1))
       • lassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂) • 
      (β ▹ π₂)) • rassociator ψ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂)
    • (ψ ◃ pair_1cell_pr2 B f l))
   • lassociator ψ π₂ l): φ · π₂ ==> ψ · π₂
ζ₁, ζ₂: ∑ γ : φ ==> ψ,
γ ▹ pb_cone_pr1 cone = α
× γ ▹ pb_cone_pr2 cone = β
((((φ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr2 B f l) ^-1)
   • lassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂) • (β ▹ π₂))
 • rassociator ψ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂)
• (ψ ◃ pair_1cell_pr2 B f l) =
pr1 ζ₁
▹ binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ c₁)) · l

          
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
l: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ (f ⊗₁ l)
(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)

 • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f)
• (ψ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
φπ₂:= fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map
  (adj_equiv_fully_faithful Hl)
  ((((((rassociator φ π₂ l
        • (φ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr2 B f l) ^-1))
       • lassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂) • 
      (β ▹ π₂)) • rassociator ψ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂)
    • (ψ ◃ pair_1cell_pr2 B f l))
   • lassociator ψ π₂ l): φ · π₂ ==> ψ · π₂
ζ₁, ζ₂: ∑ γ : φ ==> ψ,
γ ▹ pb_cone_pr1 cone = α
× γ ▹ pb_cone_pr2 cone = β
(φ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr2 B f l) ^-1)
• (lassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂
   • ((β ▹ π₂)
      • (rassociator ψ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂
         • ((ψ ◃ pair_1cell_pr2 B f l)
            • lassociator ψ π₂ l)))) =
lassociator φ π₂ l
• ((pr1 ζ₂
    ▹ binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₁ c₁))) ▹ l)

  • lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁)
 • (β ▹ π₁)) • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁ =
((lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f • (α ▹ f))
 • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f)
• (ψ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
φπ₂:= fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map
  (adj_equiv_fully_faithful Hl)
  ((((((rassociator φ π₂ l
        • (φ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr2 B f l) ^-1))
       • lassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂) • 
      (β ▹ π₂)) • rassociator ψ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂)
    • (ψ ◃ pair_1cell_pr2 B f l))
   • lassociator ψ π₂ l): φ · π₂ ==> ψ · π₂
ζ₁, ζ₂: ∑ γ : φ ==> ψ,
γ ▹ pb_cone_pr1 cone = α
× γ ▹ pb_cone_pr2 cone = β
(β ▹ π₂) • rassociator ψ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂ =
rassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂ • (pr1 ζ₂ ▹ f ⊗₁ l · π₂)

cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ (f ⊗₁ l)
(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)

Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ (f ⊗₁ l)
(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)

   • lassociator ψ π₂ l): φ · π₂ ==> ψ · π₂

 exact (pr2 (binprod_of B b₂ c₂)).

f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
l: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ (f ⊗₁ l)
(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)
q: B
φ, ψ: B ⟦ q, cone ⟧
α: φ · pb_cone_pr1 cone ==> ψ · pb_cone_pr1 cone
β: φ · pb_cone_pr2 cone ==> ψ · pb_cone_pr2 cone
p: (((φ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l) ^-1)
  • lassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₁) • 
 (β ▹ π₁)) • rassociator ψ (f ⊗₁ l) π₁ =
((lassociator φ π₁ f • (α ▹ f))
 • rassociator ψ π₁ f)
• (ψ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l) ^-1)
φπ₂:= fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map
  (adj_equiv_fully_faithful Hl)
  ((((((rassociator φ π₂ l
        • (φ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr2 B f l) ^-1))
       • lassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂) • 
      (β ▹ π₂)) • rassociator ψ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂)
    • (ψ ◃ pair_1cell_pr2 B f l))
   • lassociator ψ π₂ l): φ · π₂ ==> ψ · π₂
(adj_equiv_to_pb_ump_2_cell
 ▹ f ⊗₁ l
   · binprod_cone_pr1 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₂ c₂)))
• (is_invertible_2cell_lwhisker ψ
     (is_invertible_2cell_inv (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)))
  ^-1 =
(((φ ◃ pair_1cell_pr1 B f l) • lassociator φ π₁ f)
 • (α ▹ f)) • rassociator ψ π₁ f

B: bicat_with_binprod

α: φ · pb_cone_pr1 cone ==> ψ · pb_cone_pr1 cone
β: φ · pb_cone_pr2 cone ==> ψ · pb_cone_pr2 cone
p: (((φ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
  • lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁)
 • (β ▹ π₁)) • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr2 cone) π₁ =
((lassociator φ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f • (α ▹ f))
 • rassociator ψ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f)
• (ψ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
φπ₂:= fully_faithful_1cell_inv_map
  (adj_equiv_fully_faithful Hl)
  ((((((rassociator φ π₂ l
        • (φ ◃ (pair_1cell_pr2 B f l) ^-1))
       • lassociator φ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂) • 
      (β ▹ π₂)) • rassociator ψ (f ⊗₁ l) π₂)
    • (ψ ◃ pair_1cell_pr2 B f l))
   • lassociator ψ π₂ l): φ · π₂ ==> ψ · π₂
(adj_equiv_to_pb_ump_2_cell ▹ pb_cone_pr2 cone)
▹ binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₂ c₂)) =
β ▹ binprod_cone_pr2 (pr1 (binprod_of B b₂ c₂))
 
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
l: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ (f ⊗₁ l)
(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l)

Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ (f ⊗₁ l)
(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)
pb_ump_1 cone
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
l: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ 
  (f ⊗₁ l)
  (inv_of_invertible_2cell
     (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)
pb_ump_2 cone

      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
l: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ (f ⊗₁ l)
(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl: B ⟦ c₂, c₁ ⟧
η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)
ε:= left_equivalence_counit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell
  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)
pb_ump_1 cone
 exact adj_equiv_to_pb_ump_1.
      
B: bicat_with_binprod
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
l: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
Hl: left_adjoint_equivalence l
cone:= make_pb_cone (b₁ ⊗ c₁) π₁ (f ⊗₁ l)
(inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f l)): pb_cone f π₁

η:= left_equivalence_unit_iso Hl: invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁)
  (l · left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl)

  (left_adjoint_right_adjoint Hl · l) 
  (id₁ c₂)
pb_ump_2 cone
 exact adj_equiv_to_pb_ump_2.
    Defined.

has_pb_ump
  (make_pb_cone (pr1 (make_ar π₁)) (pr2 (make_ar π₁))
     (f ⊗₁ g)
     (inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f g)))

b₁, b₂: B

  Hg: left_adjoint_equivalence g
has_pb_ump
  (make_pb_cone (pr1 (make_ar π₁)) (pr2 (make_ar π₁))
     (f ⊗₁ g)
     (inv_of_invertible_2cell (pair_1cell_pr1 B f g)))

    apply (adj_equiv_to_pb f g g_equiv).
  Defined.

    : comprehension_bicat
    := _ ,, _ ,, trivial_comprehension_is_covariant.

    := _ ,, _ ,, trivial_comprehension_is_contravariant.
